      var activeAbs = {"62":{"c":"5","d":"95"},"66":{"a":"50","b":"50"},"67":{"a":"50","b":"50"},"68":{"b":"5","c":"95"},"70":{"a":"45","b":"45","c":"10"},"72":{"a":"50","b":"50"}};

    function runAb(name) {
        if ( !activeAbs || !activeAbs[name] ) {
            return null;
        }
        try {
            var abOpt = jQuery.parseJSON($.cookie("aboption"));
        } catch (e) {}
        if ( abOpt &amp;&amp; abOpt[name] &amp;&amp; activeAbs[name][abOpt[name]] ) {
            return abOpt[name];
        }
        var currentOpt = generateAb(activeAbs[name]);
        if ( currentOpt ) {
            recordAB(abOpt, name, currentOpt);
        }
        return currentOpt;
    }

    function recordAB(abOpt, name, currentOpt) {
        if ( !abOpt ) {
            abOpt = {};
        } else {
            $.each(abOpt, function(opt, val) {
                if ( !activeAbs[opt] ) {
                    delete abOpt[opt];
                }
            });
        }
        abOpt[name] = currentOpt;

        $.cookie("aboption", JSON.stringify(abOpt), { path: '/', domain: '.emag.ro', expires: 30 });
        $.ajax({url: "/ablogger.php?name=" + name + "&amp;value=" + currentOpt + "&amp;source=www"});

    }

    function generateAb(distribution) {
        var limit = 0;
        var rnd = Math.floor(Math.random() * 100 + 1);
        var curOpt = lastOpt = null;
        $.each(distribution, function(opt, val) {
            lastOpt = opt;
            limit+= parseFloat(val);
            if ( rnd &lt;= limit ) {
                curOpt = opt;
                return false;
            }
        });
        if ( curOpt ) {
            return curOpt;
        } else {
            return lastOpt;
        }
    }
     </script>

                                if (val.length &gt; 0) {
                                    $("div." + key + "[data-call='product_get_recommandations']").html(val);
                                    $("div." + key + "[data-call='product_get_recommandations']").attr('data-value', 'true');
                                    $("div." + key + "[data-call='product_get_recommandations']").parent().show();
                                }
                            });
                        }
                                                    if (reposition_fix) {
                                setTimeout(function() {
                                    repositioning();
                                }, 400);
                                reposition_fix = false;
                            }
                            else {
                                reposition_fix = true;
                            }

                    error: function (err) {
                    },
                    complete: function() {
                        $("div[data-call='product_get_recommandations'][data-value='false']").hide();
                        var remove_ab = ['a', 'b', 'c', 'd'];

                        var idx = remove_ab.indexOf(abOption68);

                        } else {
                            remove_ab = ['b', 'c', 'd'];

                            $('.product_reco_abcd_' + value).remove();

                            itemsFullPage: true // show only slides filled with items. default false
                        });

                    repositioning();
                }, 400);
                reposition_fix = false;
            }
            else {
                reposition_fix = true;
            }

         <script type="text/javascript">
          function CetelemComponent(options) {
    options = options || {};
    var el;
    if (!options.el || !(el = document.querySelector(options.el))) {
        return false;
    }
    options.price = options.price || 0;
    options.formattedPrice = options.formattedPrice || '&lt;span class="money-int"&gt;0&lt;/span&gt;&lt;sup class="money-decimal"&gt;00&lt;/sup&gt; &lt;span class="money-currency"&gt;Lei&lt;/span&gt;';
    options.productRate = parseFloat(options.productRate) || -1;
    options.period = options.period || 60;
    options.type = options.type || 'textOnly';

    var messages = {
        default_message: '&lt;span class="larger"&gt;Cumperi mai mult si ai dobanda mai mica!&lt;/span&gt;',
        buy_more : 'Poti sa cumperi de inca &lt;strong&gt;&lt;span class=\'money-int\'&gt;%moreWith%&lt;/span&gt; &lt;span class=\'money-currency\'&gt;Lei&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;, cu aceeasi rata lunara',
        best_offer: 'Felicitari, beneficiezi de cea mai buna oferta eCREDIT!'
    };

    var productPriceGlobal = parseFloat(options.price),
            productRate = options.productRate,
            tooltipElement,
            tooltipInnerComponent,
            barFill,
            barFillArrow,
            footerElement,
            inlineValue,
            absoluteMaximumValue = 0,
            absoluteMinimumValue = Number.MAX_VALUE;

    var cetelemCampaignData= [
        {
            productMinimumValue: 300,
            productMaximumValue: 2500,
            interest: 39, // percent
            minimumCreditPeriod: 6, // months
            maximumCreditPeriod: 60, // months
            message: messages.buy_more,
            thresholds: [
                {
                    period: 60,
                    minimum: 2080,

                },

                }

            thresholds: [

                },

                {
                    period: -1,
                    minimum: 4500,
                    maximum: 20000,
                    diff: -1,
                    message: messages.best_offer
                }
            ]
        }
    ];

    var intervalBound = 100 / cetelemCampaignData.length;

    var initElements = function() {

        switch(options.type) {
            case 'textOnly':
                el.innerHTML = '' +
                        '&lt;div class="cetelem-tooltip cetelem-text-only"&gt;' +
                        '&lt;p class="cetelem-footer"&gt;&lt;/p&gt;' +
                        '&lt;/div&gt;';

                tooltipElement = el.querySelector('.cetelem-tooltip');
                footerElement = el.querySelector('.cetelem-footer');
                break;

            case 'textGraphic':
                el.innerHTML = '' +
                        '&lt;div class="cetelem-holder"&gt;' +
                        '&lt;div class="cetelem-bar"&gt;' +
                        '&lt;div class="cetelem-bar-title"&gt;Dobanda&lt;/div&gt;' +
                        '&lt;div class="cetelem-bar-component"&gt;' +
                        '&lt;div class="cetelem-inner-component"&gt;' +
                        '&lt;div class="cetelem-bar-fill-wr"&gt;' +
                        '&lt;div class="cetelem-bar-fill"&gt;&lt;/div&gt;' +
                        '&lt;/div&gt;' +
                        '&lt;div class="cetelem-bar-arrow"&gt;&lt;/div&gt;' +
                        '&lt;div class="cetelem-inline-value"&gt;Total comanda: ' + options.formattedPrice + '&lt;/div&gt;' +
                        '&lt;/div&gt;' +
                        '&lt;/div&gt;' +
                        '&lt;/div&gt;' +
                        '&lt;p class="cetelem-footer"&gt;&lt;/p&gt;' +
                        '&lt;/div&gt;';

                tooltipElement = el.querySelector('.cetelem-tooltip');
                tooltipInnerComponent = el.querySelector('.cetelem-inner-component');
                barFill = el.querySelector('.cetelem-bar-fill');
                barFillArrow = el.querySelector('.cetelem-bar-arrow');
                footerElement = el.querySelector('.cetelem-footer');
                break;
        }
    }

    var populateTooltip = function(dataObject, productPrice, bounds, productRate) {
        var diff = dataObject.maximum - dataObject.minimum;

        footerElement.innerHTML = (dataObject.message !== undefined ? dataObject.message : dataObject.globalMessage).replace(/%moreWith%/g, diff);
        
        if (options.type == 'textGraphic') {
            if (productPrice &lt; bounds.absoluteMinimumValue) {
                percentage = 0;
            } else if (productPrice &gt;= bounds.absoluteMaximumValue){
                percentage = 100;
            } else {
                percentage = (((productPrice-bounds.productMinimumValue)/(bounds.productMaximumValue-bounds.productMinimumValue)*bounds.intervalBound))+(bounds.intervalBound*bounds.currentIndex);
            }

            // fill ecredit bar
            percentage = Math.round(percentage * 100) / 100;
            barFill.style.width = percentage + '%';
            barFillArrow.style.marginLeft = percentage + '%';
        }
    };

    var addCetelemBar = function() {
        /* create cetelem bar based on number of input intervals + find absolute minimum/maximum value  */
        for (var i = 0, len = cetelemCampaignData.length; i &lt; len; i++) {
            if (cetelemCampaignData[i].productMaximumValue &gt; absoluteMaximumValue)
                absoluteMaximumValue = cetelemCampaignData[i].productMaximumValue;
            if (cetelemCampaignData[i].productMinimumValue &lt; absoluteMinimumValue)
                absoluteMinimumValue = cetelemCampaignData[i].productMinimumValue;

            var cetelemBarPart = document.createElement('div'),
                    cetelemBarTextValue = document.createElement('div'),
                    cetelemBarVertical = document.createElement('div'),
                    cetelemBarPartText = document.createElement('div');

            cetelemBarPart.className = 'cetelem-bar-part';

            if (i === len - 1) {
                cetelemBarPart.className += ' cetelem-last-child';
            }
            cetelemBarTextValue.className = 'cetelem-bar-text-value';
            cetelemBarVertical.className = 'cetelem-bar-vertical';
            cetelemBarPartText.className = 'cetelem-bar-part-text';

            cetelemBarTextValue.appendChild(document.createTextNode(cetelemCampaignData[i].productMinimumValue.toString() + ' Lei'));
            cetelemBarPartText.appendChild(document.createTextNode(cetelemCampaignData[i].interest.toString() + '%'));

            cetelemBarPart.appendChild(cetelemBarTextValue);
            cetelemBarPart.appendChild(cetelemBarVertical);
            cetelemBarPart.appendChild(cetelemBarPartText);

            tooltipInnerComponent.appendChild(cetelemBarPart);
        }
    }

    CetelemComponent.prototype.refresh = function(productPrice, selectedCreditPeriod, productRate) {
        var thresholdObjects, thresholdObject;
        productPrice = productPrice || productPriceGlobal;
        productRate = productRate || 0;
        for (var i = 0, len = cetelemCampaignData.length; i &lt; len; i++) {
            thresholdObjects = cetelemCampaignData[i].thresholds,
                    bounds = {
                        productMinimumValue: cetelemCampaignData[i].productMinimumValue,
                        productMaximumValue: cetelemCampaignData[i].productMaximumValue,
                        absoluteMaximumValue: absoluteMaximumValue,
                        absoluteMinimumValue: absoluteMinimumValue,
                        currentIndex: i,
                        intervalBound: intervalBound
                    };

            if ((productPrice &gt;= cetelemCampaignData[i].productMinimumValue) &amp;&amp;
                    (productPrice &lt; cetelemCampaignData[i].productMaximumValue)) {
                for (var j = 0, jlen = thresholdObjects.length; j &lt; jlen - 1; j++ ){
                    thresholdObject = thresholdObjects[j];
                    thresholdObject.globalMessage = cetelemCampaignData[i].message;
                    if ((selectedCreditPeriod == thresholdObject.period) &amp;&amp;
                            (productPrice &gt;= thresholdObject.minimum) &amp;&amp;
                            (productPrice &lt; thresholdObject.maximum)) {
                        populateTooltip(thresholdObject, productPrice,bounds, productRate);
                        return;
                    }
                }
                thresholdObject = thresholdObjects[thresholdObjects.length - 1];
                thresholdObject.globalMessage = cetelemCampaignData[i].message;
                populateTooltip(thresholdObjects[thresholdObjects.length - 1], productPrice, bounds, productRate);
                return;
            }
        }

        if (productPrice &lt; absoluteMinimumValue){
            thresholdObject = thresholdObjects[0];
            thresholdObject.globalMessage = cetelemCampaignData[i].message;
            populateTooltip(thresholdObjects[0], productPrice, bounds, productRate);
            return;
        }

        thresholdObject = thresholdObjects[thresholdObjects.length - 1];
        thresholdObject.globalMessage = cetelemCampaignData[i].message;
        populateTooltip(thresholdObjects[thresholdObjects.length - 1], productPrice, bounds, productRate);
    }

    initElements();
    if (options.type == 'textGraphic') {
        addCetelemBar();
    }
    this.refresh(productPriceGlobal, options.period, productRate);
    window.x = this.refresh;
}
         </script>

Senzorul camerei principale Sony IMX135 utilizeaza sistemul RGBW ce include suplimentar un pixel alb fata de sistemul conventional RGB. Pentru autoportrete reusite sau convorbiri video cu cei dragi, ai la dispozitie o camera frontala de 5 MP cu un unghi de vizualizare impresionant.
             </p>
             <p>
              Camera principala te va surprinde zi de zi cu functiile sale inedite. Fotografii de grup, peisaje spectaculoase, poze haioase, filmari de calitate - toate acestea se vor transforma in amintiri pretioase de care te vei bucura mereu. Vei captura rapid orice moment si nu vei pierde nici un detaliu, deoarece fotografiile fiind realizate cat ai clipi.

     <script type="text/javascript">
      $(document).ready(function(){
        // set counters
        var textContent = '%left caractere ramase';
        $('#questions_add').maxlength({
            text: textContent
        });
        // end input counters

        var qSort = 'latest';
        $('#new_questions .sorting a[data-type=' + qSort + ']').addClass('selected');

        $('#new_questions .sorting a').click(function(e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            $.cookie("sortTypeQ", $(this).attr('data-type'));
            var newSort = $(this).data('type');
            if (newSort != qSort) {
                $('#new_questions .sorting a').removeClass('selected');
                $(this).addClass('selected');
                setQSort(newSort);
            }
        });

        function addAnswerMaxLength() {
            $('.adauga_raspuns_intrebare').each(function(){
                if ($(this).is(':visible') &amp;&amp; !$(this).hasClass('isMaxlength')) {
                    $(this).addClass('isMaxlength');
                    $(this).maxlength({
                        text: textContent
                    });
                }
            });
        }

        function setQSort(sort) {
            qSort = sort;
            $('#question-search-button').click();
        }

        $('#question-search').keypress(function(e){
            if (e.keyCode == 13) {
                $('#question-search-button').click();
            }
        });

        $(document).delegate('.vezi_raspunsuri', 'click', function(){
            var qid = $(this).parent().data('id');
            $('#question-' + qid).addClass('expanded');
            $('#question-' + qid).css('background-color', '#e5eef4');
            $('#question-' + qid + ' .vezi_raspunsuri').css('display', 'none');
            $('#question-' + qid + ' .raspunsuri').css('display', 'none');
            $('#question-' + qid + ' .question_caption').css('display', 'inline-block');
            $('#question-' + qid + ' .question_details').css('display', 'inline-block');
            addAnswerMaxLength();
        });

        function setMotive(){
            $('.continut_inadecvat a').each(function(){
                var bubbleId = $(this).parent().data('f');
                $(this).attr('id', 'continut' + bubbleId);
                var bubbleElement = motive(bubbleId);
                $(this).append(bubbleElement);
                $('#continut' + bubbleId).bubbletip($('#' + bubbleId + '_tooltip'), { 'deltaDirection': 'down', 'animationDuration': 10, 'delayHide': 10, 'offsetTop': -10, 'calculateOnShow': true});
            });
        }

        function motive(id_trigger){
            var motive = [{"value":"11","label":"Limbaj neadecvat"},{"value":"12","label":"Trimitere catre firma concurenta"},{"value":"13","label":"Detalii ce nu tin de produs"},{"value":"14","label":"Date personale"},{"value":"15","label":"Informatii legate de pret"},{"value":"16","label":"Sesizare"}];
            var htmlMotive = $('&lt;div&gt;', {'class': 'motive_inadecvat', 'id': id_trigger + '_tooltip', 'style':'display:none;'});
            var list = $('&lt;ul&gt;');
            for (var i = 0; i &lt; motive.length; i++) {
                list.append($('&lt;li&gt;').append($('&lt;input&gt;', {'type': 'radio', 'name': 'inadecvat[]', 'id': 'motiv-' + motive[i]['value'] + '-' + id_trigger, 'data-id': motive[i]['value']})).append($('&lt;label&gt;', {'for': 'motiv-' + motive[i]['value'] + '-' + id_trigger, 'text': motive[i]['label'] })));
            }
            htmlMotive.append(list).append($('&lt;div&gt;',{'class':'buton-nou buton-raquo trimite', 'app-id': id_trigger, 'data-p':id_trigger}).append($('&lt;span&gt;',{'class':'buton-text','text':'trimite'})));

            return htmlMotive;
        }

        function getMore(r, addTo, rewrite) {
            $.ajax({
                'url': '/product-feedback/get/', 'type': 'POST', 'dataTYpe': 'json', 'data': r,
                'success': function(data) {
                    if (rewrite == true) addTo.html(data);
                    else addTo.append(data);
                    setMotive();

                    if ( auth == 1  )
                    {
                        $('.feed_0').hide();
                        $('.feed_1').show();
                    }
                    else
                    {
                        $('.feed_1').hide();
                        $('.feed_0').show();
                    }
                }
            });
        }

        $('#question-search-button').click(function() {
            var r = { 't': 'QUESTION', 's': 0, 'l': 3, 'o': qSort, 'q': $('#question-search').val(), 'pid':420732, 'did':643695, 'fid': 4681 }
            getMore(r, $('#qcontainer'), true);
        });

        $(document).delegate('.moreq', 'click', function() {
            var r = { 't': 'QUESTION', 's': $(this).data('s'), 'l': $(this).data('l'), 'o': qSort, 'q': $('#question-search').val(), 'pid':420732, 'did':643695, 'fid': 4681 }
            $(this).remove();
            getMore(r, $('#qrowcontainer'));
        });

        $(document).delegate('.moreqa', 'click', function() {
            var r = { 't': 'ANSWER', 's': $(this).data('s'), 'l': $(this).data('l'), 'p': $(this).data('p'), 'o': qSort, 'q': $('#question-search').val(), 'pid':420732, 'did':643695, 'fid': 4681 }
            $(this).remove();
            getMore(r, $('#answersfor-' + r.p));
        });

        function showMessage(data, object) {
            var message = data.message;
            var errorCode = data.error;
            if(!errorCode){
                object.find('input[type=text]').val('');
            }
            object = object.closest('div');
            if (typeof object !== 'undefined') {
                object.block({
                    'message': '&lt;div style="padding:5px; text-align:left;font-size:12px;"&gt;' + message + '&lt;div class="buton-nou buton-raquo f-right continua"&gt;&lt;span class="buton-text"&gt;continu&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;',
                    'css':{
                        'border': '1px solid',
                        'width': '200px',
                        'z-index': 1000,
                        'background': '#fefefe',
                        'border': '1px solid #d0d0d0',
                        'border-radius': '5px',
                        'padding': '10px',
                        'margin': '0 auto',
                        'cursor' : 'normal',
                        'text-align': 'center'
                    },
                    'overlayCSS':  {
                        'cursor': 'auto',
                        'background-color':'#e8e8e8',
                        'opacity': 0.8,
                        'padding': '0px',
                        'z-index':99
                    }
                });
                $('.blockUI.blockMsg.blockElement').css('left','0').css('right','0');
                $(document).delegate('.continua', 'click', function(){
                    object.unblock();
                    if (errorCode == 0) {
                        $('.raspunde_primul[data-p="' + object.data('p') + '"]').replaceWith($('&lt;p&gt;',{'text':message}));
                    }
                });
            }
        }


            function add(r, object) {
                $.ajax({
                    'url': '/product-feedback/add/?' + r.t, 'type': 'POST', 'dataTYpe': 'json', 'data': r,
                    'success': function(data) {
                        showMessage(data, object);
                    }
                });
            }

            $('#questions_add_button').click(function() {
                var message = $('#questions_add').val();
                if (!message.length) {
                    showMessage({'error':1, 'message': "Te rugam sa completezi intrebarea!"}, $(this).parent());
                    return;
                }
                var r = { 't': 'QUESTION', 'pid':420732, 'did':643695, 'fid':4681, 'msg': message }
                add(r, $('#add_question'));
                $('#questions_add').val('').trigger('change');
                var dataC = new Date();
                var dataExp = dataC.setTime(dataC.getTime() + (3*60*1000));
                $.cookie("save_caption", 'null', {expires: dataExp, path: '/'});
            });


            $('#questions_add').keypress(function(e) {
                if (e.keyCode == 13) {
                    $('#questions_add_button').click();
                }
            });
            $(document).delegate('.adauga_raspuns_intrebare', 'keypress', function(e) {
                if (e.keyCode == 13) {
                    $('#answer_add_button').click();
                }
            });

            $(document).delegate('#answer_add_button', 'click', function() {
                var message = $('.adauga_raspuns_intrebare[data-p="' + $(this).data('p') + '"]').val();
                if (!message.length) {
                    showMessage({'error':1, 'message': "Te rugam sa completezi raspunsul!"}, $(this).parent());
                    return;
                }
                var r = { 't': 'ANSWER', 'pid':420732, 'did':643695, 'fid':4681, 'p': $(this).data('p'), 'msg': message }
                add(r, $(this).parent());
                $('.adauga_raspuns_intrebare[data-p="' + $(this).data('p') + '"]').val('').trigger('change');
            });



        $(document).delegate('.answer_util_da', 'click', function() {
            var r = { 'f': $(this).data('f') };
            var o = $(this).parent().children('.caption');
            var b = $(this);
            $.ajax({
                'url': '/product-feedback/vote/', 'type': 'POST', 'dataType': 'json', 'data': r,
                'success': function(data) {
                    if (!data.error) {
                        o.html(data.message);
                        b.remove();
                    }
                    else{
                        showMessage(data, o.parent());
                    }
                }
            });
        });

        function getMotive() {
            return [{"value":"11","label":"Limbaj neadecvat"},{"value":"12","label":"Trimitere catre firma concurenta"},{"value":"13","label":"Detalii ce nu tin de produs"},{"value":"14","label":"Date personale"},{"value":"15","label":"Informatii legate de pret"},{"value":"16","label":"Sesizare"}];
        }


        $(document).delegate('.raspunde_primul', 'click', function(){
            $('.raspunde_primul').show();
            $('.right .question_row .raspunde').hide();
            $(this).parent("div").children(".raspunde").show();
            $(this).hide();
            addAnswerMaxLength();
        });

        $(document).delegate('.save_caption', 'click', function(){
            if($(this).attr('data-t') == 'add'){
                if (!$('#questions_add').val().length) { showMessage({'error':1, 'message': "Te rugam sa completezi intrebarea!"}, $(this).parent()); return; }
                var caption = $('#questions_add').attr('data-p') + '|' + $('#questions_add').val();
                var dataC = new Date();
                var dataExp = dataC.setTime(dataC.getTime() + (3*60*1000));

                $.cookie("save_caption", caption, {expires: dataExp, path: '/'});
                window.location.href = '/user/login?redirect_key=/telefon-mobil-allview-black-x2-soul/pd/DHRVLBBBM/%23questions_add';
            }
            else{
                var caption = $('#adauga_raspuns_intrebare_'+$(this).attr('data-p')).attr('data-p') + '|' + $('#adauga_raspuns_intrebare_'+$(this).attr('data-p')).val();
                var dataC = new Date();
                var dataExp = dataC.setTime(dataC.getTime() + (3*60*1000));
                $.cookie("save_caption", caption, {expires: dataExp, path: '/'});
                window.location.href = '/user/login?redirect_key='+$(this).attr('data-l');
            }
        });
        var save_caption = $.cookie("save_caption");
        if (save_caption != 'null' &amp;&amp; save_caption != null &amp;&amp; save_caption) {
            save_caption = save_caption.split('|');
            if (typeof save_caption[0] !== 'undefined') {
                $('input[data-p="' + save_caption[0] + '"]').val(save_caption[1]);
                $('#questions_add_button').trigger('click');
                var dataC = new Date();
                var dataExp = dataC.setTime(dataC.getTime() + (3*60*1000));
                $.cookie("save_caption", 'null', {expires: dataExp, path: '/'});
            }
        }


                                    $('.intrebari').html('16');
                        $('.intrebari').show();
        

    });

    $111(window).load(function() {
        var $questionInput = $111('#question-search'),
            $questionButton = $111('#question-search-button'),
            $iconClose = $111('.question-search-wr .js-icon-close');

        var checkInput = function() {
            if ($questionInput.val() === '') {
                $iconClose.hide();
            } else {
                $iconClose.show();
            }
        };

        $questionInput.on('change', checkInput);
        $questionInput.on('keyup', checkInput);
        $questionInput.on('focus', checkInput);
        $questionInput.on('blur', checkInput);
        $questionInput.on('mousedown', checkInput);

        $iconClose.on('click', function() {
            $questionInput.val('');
            $iconClose.hide();
            $questionButton.trigger('click');
        });

    });

         </div>
         <div class="review_pentru">
          Review pentru: Telefon mobil Allview X2 Soul, Black
         </div>
         <div class="review_body review_body_truncated" style="max-height:66px;overflow:hidden;">
          Am cumparat acest telefon de la emag si l-am dus inapoi dupa aproximativ o saptamana. Este un telefon al extremelor ce lasa mult de dorit pe partea hardware. In primul rand trebuie sa laud aspectul fizic. Telefonul are sticla pe fata si spate este foarte subtire si usor si se simte incredibil in...
         </div>
         <div class="review_body review_body_full" style="display: none">
          Am cumparat acest telefon de la emag si l-am dus inapoi dupa aproximativ o saptamana. Este un telefon al extremelor ce lasa mult de dorit pe partea hardware. In primul rand trebuie sa laud aspectul fizic. Telefonul are sticla pe fata si spate este foarte subtire si usor si se simte incredibil in mana, Absolut nimic de reprosat aici. Este unul dintre cele mai frumoase telefoane pe care le-am avut. Seamana mult cu zperia z, dar este mai subtire si un pic mai elegant. Desi stiam ca este aproximativ acelasi ecran ca si pe Samsung s4, mi-a depasit asteptarile. Strict din punctul meu de vedere ecranul este mai bun decat cel de pe s4. Culorile si detaliile parca se vad un pic mai bine. Din punct de vedere audio este cat se poate de mediocru atat la difuzorul extern cat si la casti. Castile sunt ok, nu ma pot plange, dar nu se compara spre exemplu cu o pereche de sony sau pioneer la sub 100 Ron. Nu stiu exact daca amplificatorul Yamaha este doar o strategie de marketing dar eu nu am fost deloc impresionat de difozor. Se aude decent si atat. Partea interesanta este hardware-ul si de aici si cele 3 stele acordate. In primul rand se incinge extrem de tare. Dupa 5 min de folosit, nu jucat, incepe sa se incalzeasca destul de serios. Dupa doar 10 min de gaming telefoul arde efectiv si devine foarte dificil de tinut in mana. Nu am cumparat telefonul sa ma joc dar totusi sa se incalzeazca asa rau dupa cateva minute de browsing si citit mail-uri nu mi se pare ok. Proceserul si GPU-ul par super ok pe hartie si telefonul chiar se misca excelent prin meniuri, browsing, facebook, etc. Nu am simtiti decat un pic de lag cand aveam mai multe aplicatii pornite, dar nimic care sa afecteze experienta de utilizare. Pentru gameri nu recomand totusi acest telefon. Trebuie avut in vedere ca jocurile de ultima generatie precum Asphalt 8, Modern Combat 5, GTA San Andrea si Vice City etc. NU merg pe aceasta configuratie, Am vazut ca circula pe net anumite versiuni adaptate pentru aceasta configuratie dar sunt pline de bug-uri. Baterie mai slaba ca pe allview nu am mai intalnit. Nu duce nici macar 12 ore de utilizre moderata. Si aici ma refer la wi-fi si data always on, cateva apeluri si sms-uri. Aprox 30-40 de min de fb si whatsapp si 1 ora de muzica cu ecranul oprit. La mine a dus maxim 11h30min de la 100% la 0%. Wi-fi-ul este foarte slab. In living, cu orice alt device am semanal aproape full, dar cu x2-ul nu reauseam sa am nici o liniuta si de cele mai multe ori era picat. Mentionez ca router-ul wireless este la o distanta de aproximativ 10m si sunt 2 pereti intre el si living. Camera fotovare un pic de lag dar face poze super ok. Nu am nimic de comentat. Face ce trebuie. Video nu am testat. Cel mai aiurea aspect la toata povestea este semanlul. De cel putin 2-3 ori pe zi ramaneam fara semanal. Am vb la allview si mi-au zis ca semnal am si ca este doar un bug de software. Nimic mai fals, deoarce nu puteam sa intiez si sa primesc apeluri. Am citit pe softpedia despre acasta probela si am vazut ca nu sunt singurul, si ca allview are acelasi raspuns pentru toti. Poate ca totusi exista si posesori de x2 care nu au acasta problema si au fost doar cateva aparate cu problema. In concluzie, procesorul, bateria si supra-incalzirea m-au facut sa renunt la telefon, chiar daca este incredibil de frumos.
         </div>

     <script type="text/javascript">
      var translations = translations || {};
    translations.reviews = translations.reviews || {};
    translations.reviews.abouttext = 'eMAG - Online va fi mereu simplu';
    translations.reviews.pause = 'Pauza';
    translations.reviews.play = 'Start';
    
    function reviews_f(auth) {
        // set review comment counter
        var textContent = '%left caractere ramase';
        $('.review_comment').maxlength({
            text: textContent
        });

        $('.add_comment').maxlength({
            text: textContent
        });
        // end counter

        $(document).delegate('.review_read_more', 'click', function(){
            $(this).parent().find('.review_body.review_body_truncated').remove();
            $(this).parent().find('.review_body.review_body_full').show();
            $(this).hide();
        });

        $(document).delegate('.question_read_more', 'click', function(){
            $(this).parent().find('.question_body').attr('style','max-height: none !important;');
            $(this).hide();
            $(this).next('br').remove();
        });

        $('.reviw_com_btn').each(function(){
            if($(this).parent().children('p').children('span').height() &gt; 50){
                $(this).show();
            }
        });
        $(document).delegate('.reviw_com_btn', 'click', function(){
            if($(this).parent().children('p').children('span').height() &gt; 50){
                $(this).hide();
                $(this).parent().children('p').attr('style', '');
            }
        });

        $('.review_images_carusel').show();
        $(document).delegate('#scrie_review', 'click', function() {
            if(!$('#add_review').hasClass('open')){
                if(typeof init_add_review_plugins == 'function'){
                    init_add_review_plugins();
                }

                $(this).removeClass('on').addClass('off');
                $('#add_review').fadeIn();
                $('#add_review').addClass('open');
            }
            else{
                $('#add_review').removeClass('open');
                $(this).removeClass('off').addClass('on');
                $('#add_review').fadeOut();
            }
        });
        var rSort = 'popularity';
        $('#new_reviews .sorting a[data-type=' + rSort + ']').addClass('selected');

        $('#new_reviews .sorting a').click(function(e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            $.cookie("sortTypeR", $(this).data('type'));
            var newSort = $(this).data('type');
            if (newSort != rSort) {
                $('#new_reviews .sorting a').removeClass('selected');
                $(this).addClass('selected');
                setRSort(newSort);
            }
        });
        function setRSort(sort) {
            rSort = sort;
            $('#reviews-search-button').click();
        }

        $('#reviews-search').keypress(function(e){
            if (e.keyCode == 13) {
                $('#reviews-search-button').click();
            }
        });

        function getMoreR(r, addTo, rewrite) {
            $.ajax({
                'url': '/product-feedback/get/',
                'type': 'POST',
                'dataTYpe': 'json',
                'data': r,
                'success': function(data) {
                    if (rewrite == true) addTo.html(data);
                    else addTo.append(data);
                    setMotive();
                }
            });
        }

        $('#reviews-search-button').click(function() {
            var r = { 't': 'REVIEW', 's': 0, 'l': 3, 'o': rSort, 'q': $('#reviews-search').val(), 'pid':420732, 'did':643695, 'fid': 4681 };
            getMoreR(r, $('#rcontainer'), true);
        });

        $(document).delegate('.more_r', 'click', function() {
            var r = { 't': 'REVIEW', 's': $(this).data('s'), 'l': $(this).data('l'), 'o': rSort, 'q': $('#reviews-search').val(), 'pid':420732, 'did':643695, 'fid': 4681 }
            $(this).remove();
            getMoreR(r, $('#rcontainer'));
        });

        $(document).delegate('.more_c', 'click', function() {
            var r = { 't': 'COMMENT', 's': $(this).data('s'), 'l': $(this).data('l'), 'p': $(this).data('p'), 'o': rSort, 'pid':420732, 'did':643695, 'fid': 4681 }
            $(this).remove();
            getMoreR(r, $('#commentsfor-' + r.p));
        });

        $(document).delegate('.more_c_c', 'click', function() {
            var r = { 't': 'COMMENT', 'p': $(this).data('p'), 'l': $(this).data('l'), 'pid':420732, 'fid': 4681 }
            $(this).remove();
            getMoreR(r, $('#c_commentsfor-' + r.p), true);
        });

        function add(r, object){
            $.ajax({
                'url': '/product-feedback/add/?' + r.t,
                'type': 'POST',
                'dataTYpe': 'json',
                'data': r,
                'success': function(data) {
                    showMessage(data, object);
                }
            });
        }

        function showMessage(data, object) {
            var message = data.message;
            var errorCode = data.error;
            if (typeof object !== 'undefined') {
                object.block({
                    'message': '&lt;div style="padding:5px; text-align:left;font-size:12px;display: inline;"&gt;' + message + '&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class="buton-nou buton-raquo f-right" id="inchide"&gt;&lt;span class="buton-text" id="review_show_m"&gt;intra in cont&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;',
                    'css':{
                        'border': '1px solid',
                        'width': '200px',
                        'z-index': 1000,
                        'background': '#fefefe',
                        'border': '1px solid #d0d0d0',
                        'border-radius': '5px',
                        'padding': '10px',
                        'margin': '0 auto',
                        'cursor' : 'normal',
                        'text-align': 'center'
                    },
                    'overlayCSS':  {
                        'cursor': 'auto',

        $(document).delegate('.add_review_comment', 'click', function() {

            if ( auth == 0 )
            {
                var caption = $(this).attr('data-p')+'|' + $('.review_comment[data-p="' + $(this).data('p') + '"]').val();
                var dataC = new Date();
                var dataExp = dataC.setTime(dataC.getTime() + (3*60*1000));
                $.cookie("save_caption_review", caption, {expires: dataExp, path: '/'});
                window.location.href = '/user/login?redirect_key='+$(this).attr('data-l');
            }
            else
            {
                var message = $('.review_comment[data-p="' + $(this).data('p') + '"]').val();
                if (!message.length) {
                    showMessage({'error':1, 'message': "Te rugam sa completezi comentariul!"}, $(this).parent());
                    return;
                }
                var r = { 't': 'COMMENT', 'pid':420732, 'did':643695, 'fid':4681, 'p': $(this).data('p'), 'msg': message }
                add(r, $(this).parent());
                $('.review_comment[data-p="' + $(this).data('p') + '"]').val('').trigger('change');
            }
        });

        $(document).delegate('.review-util-vot', 'click', function() {
            var r = { 'f': $(this).data('f') };
            var o = $(this).parent().children('.caption');
            var b = $(this);
            $.ajax({
            'url': '/product-feedback/vote/', 'type': 'POST', 'dataTYpe': 'json', 'data': r,
                'success': function(data) {
                    if (!data.error) {
                        o.html(data.message);
                        b.remove();
                    }
                    else{
                        showMessage(data, o.parent());
                    }
                }
            });
        });

        function setMotive(){
            $('.continut_inadecvat a').each(function(){
                var bubbleId = $(this).parent().data('f');
                $(this).attr('id', 'continut' + bubbleId);
                var bubbleElement = motive(bubbleId);
                $(this).append(bubbleElement);
                $('#continut' + bubbleId).bubbletip($('#' + bubbleId + '_tooltip'), { 'deltaDirection': 'down', 'animationDuration': 10, 'delayHide': 10, 'offsetTop': -10, 'calculateOnShow': true});
            });
        }
        setMotive();

        function motive(id_trigger){
            var motive = [{"value":"11","label":"Limbaj neadecvat"},{"value":"12","label":"Trimitere catre firma concurenta"},{"value":"13","label":"Detalii ce nu tin de produs"},{"value":"14","label":"Date personale"},{"value":"15","label":"Informatii legate de pret"},{"value":"16","label":"Sesizare"}];
            var htmlMotive = $('&lt;div&gt;', {'class': 'motive_inadecvat', 'id': id_trigger + '_tooltip', 'style':'display:none;'});
            var list = $('&lt;ul&gt;');
            for (var i = 0; i &lt; motive.length; i++) {
                list.append($('&lt;li&gt;').append($('&lt;input&gt;', {'type': 'radio', 'name': 'inadecvat[]', 'id': 'motiv-' + motive[i]['value'] + '-' + id_trigger, 'data-id': motive[i]['value']})).append($('&lt;label&gt;', {'for': 'motiv-' + motive[i]['value'] + '-' + id_trigger, 'text': motive[i]['label'] })));
            }
            htmlMotive.append(list).append($('&lt;div&gt;',{'class':'buton-nou buton-raquo trimite', 'app-id': id_trigger, 'data-p':id_trigger}).append($('&lt;span&gt;',{'class':'buton-text','text':'trimite'})));

            return htmlMotive;
        }

        $(document).delegate('.motive_inadecvat .trimite', 'click', function(){
            var feedback_id = $(this).attr('app-id');
            var report_id = $('.motive_inadecvat input[type=radio]:checked').attr('data-id');
            if (typeof report_id !== 'undefined'){
                $.ajax({
                    'url': '/product-feedback/report/',
                    'type': 'POST',
                    'datatype': 'json',
                    'data': { f: feedback_id, r: report_id },
                    'success': function(data) {
                        if (!data.error) {
                            $('#continut' + feedback_id).removeBubbletip();
                            $('#continut' + feedback_id).parent().html(('&lt;span style="color:#959595;font-size:12px;"&gt;'+data.message+'&lt;/span&gt;'));
                        }
                    }
                });
            } else {
                alert('Alege un criteriu pentru continut inadecvat !');
            }
        });

        $reviewsInput.on('blur', checkInput);
        $reviewsInput.on('mousedown', checkInput);

            $reviewsInput.val('');
            $iconClose.hide();
            $reviewsButton.trigger('click');

    <script type="text/javascript">
     function repositioning(where){
        var scrollToElement = false;
        if (typeof where !== 'undefined' &amp;&amp; where !== '') {
            var currentElement = where;
        } else {
            var currentElement = window.location.hash.replace('!','');
            scrollToElement = false;
        }

        if(typeof currentElement !== 'undefined' &amp;&amp; currentElement !== '') {
            switch(currentElement) {
                case '#add_review':
                    $('#scrie_review.on').click();
                    if($(window).height() &gt; 700) currentElement = '#new_reviews';
                    scrollToElement = true;
                    break;
                case '#top':
                    $("html, body").stop().animate({scrollTop: 0}, 'slow');
                    break;
                default:
                    break;
            }

            if ($(currentElement).length) {
                var $butonCurrentElement = $('#but_' + currentElement.replace('#', ''));
                var butonCEoffset = 0;
                if ($butonCurrentElement.length) {
                    butonCEoffset = parseInt($butonCurrentElement.offset().top) - $('#bannerMenuReviews').offset().top + 20;
                }

                                var reposition = parseInt($(currentElement).offset().top) - butonCEoffset - 170;
                                if (scrollToElement) {
                    reposition = parseInt($(currentElement).offset().top) - 50;
                }

                $('html,body').animate({scrollTop: reposition}, 'slow');
            }
        }
    }

    $(window).load(function() {
        var lastId,
            $sidebar = $("#bannerMenuReviews"),
            $noOfQuestions = $sidebar.find('.js-questions'),
            $noOfReviews = $sidebar.find('.js-reviews'),
            $menuItems = $sidebar.find("a"),
            $up = $sidebar.find('.sidebar-up'),
            $productInfo = $('#product-pictures-content'),
            offsetHeight = -50 + $productInfo.offset().top + $productInfo.height(),
            sidebarHeight = $sidebar.outerHeight() + 10,
            $sidebarDescription = $sidebar.find('#but_description_section'),
            $descriptionSection = $('#description_section'),
            $scrollItems = $menuItems.map(function() {
                var item = $($(this).attr("href"));
                if (item.length) {
                    return item;
                }
            });
        $sidebar.css("top", offsetHeight + "px");
        $sidebar.show();

        var onScrollFunction = function() {
            // Get container scroll position
            if ($(document).scrollTop() &gt; offsetHeight - 200) {
                $sidebar.addClass('sidebar-fixed');
            } else {
                $sidebar.removeClass('sidebar-fixed');
            }

            var cur = $scrollItems.map(function() {
                var $this = $(this),
                    bottomElement = $sidebar.find('#but_' + $this.attr('id')).offset().top;
                if ($this.offset().top &lt; bottomElement &amp;&amp; ($this.offset().top + $this.height()) &gt; bottomElement) {
                    return this;
                }
            });

            cur = cur[cur.length - 1];
            var id = cur &amp;&amp; cur.length ? cur[0].id : "";
            
            if ($sidebarDescription.offset().top &lt; $descriptionSection.offset().top) {
                $up.addClass('invisible');
            } else {
                $up.removeClass('invisible');
            }
            if (lastId !== id) {
                lastId = id;
                $sidebar.find('&gt;a').removeClass("selected");
                if (lastId !== '') {
                    $sidebar.find('#but_' + lastId).addClass("selected");
                }
            }
        }

        $(window).scroll(onScrollFunction);
        
        // trigger a scroll event to make the initial check
        onScrollFunction();

        $("#bannerMenuReviews a, .total_reviews").click(function(e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            repositioning($(this).attr('href'));
        });

            });
    </script>

        function validateProductService() {
            var selectedService = this;
            $(".productServicesChoiceBox .input_extra_warranty").each(function(k, v) {
                if($(selectedService).val() != $(v).val()) {
                    $(v).removeAttr("checked");
                } else {
                    if( selectedService.checked ) {
                        $(v).attr("checked", "checked");
                    } else {
                        $(v).removeAttr("checked");
                    }
                }
            });

            var serviceElement = document.getElementById("extra_warranty_" + $(this).val() ).checked;
            //var elementID = "extra_warranty_" + $(this).val();
            if( serviceElement ) {
                $(".productServicesChoiceBox .narrowed .info").html($(this).parent().html().replace(/(&lt;input (.*)&gt;)/,"&lt;input type='checkbox' name='service[]' class='input_extra_warranty' checked='checked' value='"+$(this).val()+"'&gt;").replace('Plus ','+'));
                $(".productServicesChoiceBox .narrowed .info .warranty-info").remove();
                $(".productServicesChoiceBox .narrowed .info .productService-info").remove();
                $(".productServicesChoiceBox .narrowed .info input").attr("checked", "checked");
                $(".productServicesChoiceBox .narrowed").show();
                $(".productServicesChoiceBox .expanded").hide();
            } else {
                $(".productServicesChoiceBox .narrowed .info input").val($(".productServicesChoiceBox .input_extra_warranty").eq(0).val());
                $(".productServicesChoiceBox .narrowed .info label").attr("for","extra_warranty_"+$(".productServicesChoiceBox .input_extra_warranty").eq(0).val());
                $(".productServicesChoiceBox .narrowed .info label").html("").append($(".productServicesChoiceBox .input_extra_warranty").eq(0).parent().children("label span").html()).append($(".productServicesChoiceBox .input_extra_warranty").eq(0).parent().children("label").html().replace(/(&lt;input (.*)&gt;&lt;\/span&gt;)/,""));
            }

            $(".productServicesChoiceBox .input_extra_warranty").unbind("change");
            $(".productServicesChoiceBox .input_extra_warranty").change(validateProductService);
        }

	    function displayPseudoClose() {
	        $('#product-offers #resealed-offers tr').each( function( index ) {
	            if(index &lt; 2){
	                $(this).css('display', 'table-row');
	                if(index == 1){
	                    $(this).find('td').css('overflow', 'hidden');
	                    $(this).css('overflow', 'hidden');
	                    $(this).find('td').css('height', '40px');
	                    $(this).css('height', '40px');
	                }
	            }else{
	                $(this).css('display', 'none');
	                $(this).find('td').css('overflow', '');
	                $(this).css('overflow', '');
	                $(this).find('td').css('height', '');
	                $(this).css('height', '');
	            }
	        });

	        $('#product-offers #resealed-continer').css('height', '130px');
	        $('#product-offers #resealed-continer').css('overflow', 'hidden');
	    }

			function getZoomAreaPosition() {
				var imgX = $("#zoom-image img").width();
				var imgY = $("#zoom-image img").height();
				var viewX = 525;
				var viewY = 350;
				var zoomX = viewX * 100 / imgX;
				var zoomY = viewY * 100 / imgY;
				var areaX = zoomX / 100 * 350;
				var areaY = zoomY / 100 * 350;
				var offsetX = (nx * 100 / imgX ) / 100 * 350;
				var offsetY = (ny * 100 / imgY ) / 100 * 350;

				var x = qst.pageX - (areaX / 2);
				var y = qst.pageY - (areaY / 2);

				if (x &lt; imgPosition.topX) x = imgPosition.topX;
				if (y &lt; imgPosition.topY) y = imgPosition.topY;

				if (x + areaX &gt; imgPosition.bottomX) x = x - (x + areaX - imgPosition.bottomX);
				if (y + areaY &gt; imgPosition.bottomY) y = y - (y + areaY - imgPosition.bottomY);

				var top = y;
				var left = x;

				return {'areaX' : parseInt(areaX), 'areaY' : parseInt(areaY), 'top' : parseInt(top), 'left' : parseInt(left) }
			}
			function getZoomArea() {
				// zoom area
				var position = getZoomAreaPosition();
				var zoom = $('&lt;div&gt;',{ 'id' : 'zoomArea' });
				zoom.css('position','absolute');
				zoom.css('background-color','none');
				zoom.css('border','2px solid red');
				zoom.css('width',position.areaX+'px');
				zoom.css('height',position.areaY+'px');
				zoom.css('top',position.top+'px');
				zoom.css('left',position.left+'px');
				zoom.css('cursor','url("http://s1emagst.akamaized.net/layout/ro/images/new/cursor_zoom.png") 5 8, default');
				zoom.click(function(){ $("#product-pictures-picture .poza_produs").click(); });
				return zoom;
			}
			function moveZoomArea() {
				var position = getZoomAreaPosition();
				$('#zoomArea').css('top',position.top+'px');
				$('#zoomArea').css('left',position.left+'px');
			}

			var nx = 0;
			var ny = 0;
			function trackZoom(event){
				if (!event || !event.pageX) event = qst;
				var x = event.pageX - imgPosition.topX;
				var y = event.pageY - imgPosition.topY;
				var rx = x / 350;
				var ry = y / 350;

				nx = parseInt($("#zoom-image").width()) / 2 - parseInt($("#zoom-image img").width()) * rx;
				ny = parseInt($("#zoom-image").height()) / 2 - parseInt($("#zoom-image img").height()) * ry;

				if ($("#zoom-image img").width() + nx &lt; $("#zoom-image").width()) nx = 0 - $("#zoom-image img").width() + $("#zoom-image").width();
				if ($("#zoom-image img").height() + ny &lt; $("#zoom-image").height()) ny = 0 - $("#zoom-image img").height() + $("#zoom-image").height();
				if (nx &gt; 0) nx = 0;
				if (ny &gt; 0) ny = 0;

				$("#zoom-image img").css("left",nx + "px");
				$("#zoom-image img").css("top",ny + "px");

				moveZoomArea();
			}

	        // Initial call for psudo promo box
			displayPseudoClose();
            displayPseudoClosePromo();
			displayPseudoCloseResealed();
			$('#product-subproducts').mouseenter(function() {
			    subproducts = true;
			});
			$('#product-subproducts').mouseleave(function() {
			    subproducts = false;
			});

			$(document).mousemove(function(e) {
				qst = e;

				if (
						e.pageX &gt;= imgPosition.topX
						&amp;&amp; e.pageX &lt;= imgPosition.bottomX
						&amp;&amp; e.pageY &gt;= imgPosition.topY
						&amp;&amp; e.pageY &lt;= imgPosition.bottomY
						&amp;&amp; $(e.target).closest('.blockOverlay').length == 0
						&amp;&amp; $('.extra-warranty-question').length == 0
                        &amp;&amp; $('#emg-mega-menu.open').length == 0
						&amp;&amp; $('.emg-modal').length == 0
						&amp;&amp; $(e.target).closest('#object-360').length == 0
						&amp;&amp; $(e.target).closest('#autoModalContainer').length == 0
                        //&amp;&amp; $(e.target).closest('#productPdfPreview').length == 0
						&amp;&amp; !subproducts
                        &amp;&amp; !$('#bundle-first-thumb, #object-360-thumb').hasClass('active')
                        &amp;&amp; $('#productPdfPreview').length == 0
					) {
					if (!zoomed) {
						zoomed = true;
						if (z) {
							clearTimeout(z);
							z = null;
						}
                        if( $('#suggestLayer').css('display') == 'none' ) {
                            z = setTimeout(function(){
                                $("#zoom-image-container").show();
                                if($('#zoom-image img').width()&lt;1000){
                                    $("#zoom-image-container").hide();
                                    return;
                                }
                                $('#special-badge').css('visibility','hidden');
                                $('#comparator').css('visibility','hidden');
                                //$("#product-subproducts").hide();
                                $("#product-subproducts").css("visibility","hidden");
                                zoom = getZoomArea();
                                $('#product-pictures-picture div.poza-mare-produs').append(zoom);
                                trackZoom(qst,$("#product-pictures-picture .poza_produs img"));
                                z = null;
                            },400);
                        }
					} else {
                        //when hovering with mouse recalculate the position everytime so it won't go outside the div
                        computeInitialPosition();
						trackZoom(qst,$("#product-pictures-picture .poza_produs img"));
					}
				} else {
					if (zoomed) {
						if (z) {
							clearTimeout(z);
							z = null;
						}
						$("#zoom-image-container").hide();
						//$("#product-subproducts").show();
						$("#product-subproducts").css("visibility","visible");
						$('#zoomArea').remove();
						zoomed = false;

						$('#special-badge').css('visibility','visible');
						$('#comparator').css('visibility','visible');
					}
				}
			});

		});

		var t = 0;
		$('#object-360').mouseenter(function(){
			t = setTimeout(function(){
				if(!subproducts){
					$("#product-subproducts").css("visibility","hidden");
				}
			},400);
		});
		$('#object-360').mouseleave(function(){
			clearTimeout(t);
			$("#product-subproducts").css("visibility","visible");
		});


        $("#product-pictures-picture .poza_produs, #product-bundle-holder .poza_produs").click(function(e) {
            e.stopPropagation();
            e.preventDefault();
            var a = $('#mycarousel .jcarousel-item.active');
            if (!a.length) a = $('#mycarousel .jcarousel-item:first');
            a.children('a').click();
        });

        var viewMorePromo = false;
	    $('#product-promos .narrowed, #product-promos .more-less-button').click(function(){
	        if( /*$('#product-promos .narrowed').length &gt; 0*/ !viewMorePromo){
	            $('#product-promos .narrowed').removeClass("narrowed").addClass("expanded");
	            $('#vodafone-offers-holder').css({height: 'auto'});

	            $('.other_bundle').css('display','block');
	            $('#product-promos .more-less-button').html("vezi mai putine");
	            $('#product-promos form').css('overflow', '');
	            $('#product-promos form').css('height', '');
	            viewMorePromo = true;
	            $('#more_bundles_fade').hide();
	        } else {
	            $('#product-promos .expanded').removeClass("expanded").addClass("narrowed");
	            $('#product-promos .more-less-button').html("vezi mai multe");

	            	            $('#vodafone-offers-holder').height($('#vodafone-offers tr:first-child').outerHeight(true) + $('#more_bundles_fade').outerHeight(true));

	        }

        $(document).ready(function () {
            var t = null;
            $("#mycarousel .jcarousel-item").mouseenter(function(){
                if (t) {
                    clearTimeout(t);
                    t = null;
                }
                var that = this;
                t = setTimeout(function() {
                    if($('#object-360').length &gt; 0 &amp;&amp; $(that).attr('id') == 'object-360-thumb'){
                        $('#object-360').css('display', 'block');
                        $("#product-pictures-picture .poza_produs").css('display', 'none');
                        $('#product-bundle-holder').hide();
                        $('#productPdfPreview').css('display', 'none');
                    }else if($('#object-360-sec').length &gt; 0 &amp;&amp; $(that).attr('id') == 'object-360-thumb-sec'){
                        $('#object-360').css('display', 'block');
                        $("#product-pictures-picture .poza_produs").css('display', 'none');
                        $('#product-bundle-holder').hide();
                        $('#productPdfPreview').css('display', 'none');
                    }else if($('#bundle-first-thumb').length &gt; 0 &amp;&amp; $(that).attr('id') == 'bundle-first-thumb'){
                        $("#product-pictures-picture .bundle-picture").show();
                        $("#product-pictures-picture .poza_produs").hide();
                        $('#object-360').hide();
                        $('#product-bundle-holder').show();
                        $('#productPdfPreview').css('display', 'none');
                    }else if($('#pic-thumb').length &gt; 0 &amp;&amp; $(that).attr('id') == 'pic-thumb'){
                        $("#product-pictures-picture .poza_produs").attr("src",$(that).children("a").attr("data-original"));
                        $("#product-pictures-picture .poza-mare-produs a").attr("href",$(that).children("a").attr("data-original"));
                        $("#zoom-image img").attr("src",$(that).children("a").attr("data-original"));
                        $('#product-bundle-holder').hide();

                        $("#product-pictures-picture .poza_produs").css('display', 'block');
                        $('#object-360').css('display', 'none');
                        $('#productPdfPreview').css('display', 'none');
                     } else if($('#productPdfPreview').length &gt; 0 &amp;&amp; $(that).attr('id') == 'pdf-preview-thumb') {
                         $('#object-360').css('display', 'none');
                         $("#product-pictures-picture .poza_produs").css('display', 'none');
                         $('#product-bundle-holder').hide();
                         $('#productPdfPreview').css('display', 'block');
                         $('#productPdfPreview .poza_produs').css('display', 'block');

                    }
                    computeInitialPosition();

                    $('.jcarousel-item').removeClass('active');
                    $(that).addClass('active');
                    t = null;
                },100);
            });

            $("#mycarousel .jcarousel-item").mouseleave(function(){
                if (t) {
                    clearTimeout(t);
                    t = null;
                }
            });

        });

  <script>
   window.nrlskOnEvent = function(padiact)
{	
	if (padiact.type == 'open')
	{
        if (padiact.id == 9272){

            $('&lt;link rel="stylesheet" href="/resources/css/padiact/ro/'+padiact.id+'.css" type="text/css" /&gt;').appendTo('head');

            if ( $('.padiFormWrap ul').length &gt; 0 ){
                // Get Exising Select Options
                $('.padiFormWrap ul').each(function(i, ul){
                    var $ul = $(ul);
                    var $p = $("&lt;p/&gt;");
                    $ul.find('label').each(function(j, label){
                        var $label = $(label);
                        if ($label.hasClass("padiLabel")){
                            $p.append("&lt;label class='padiLabel'&gt;&lt;span&gt;"+$label.text()+"&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/label&gt;");
                        }
                        else{
                            // Create a radio:
                            var $checkbox = $('&lt;input type="checkbox" /&gt;');
                            // Set name and value:
                            $checkbox.attr({
                                name: $label.children(":first").attr('name'),
                                id: $label.children(":first").attr('id'),
                                value: $label.children(":first").attr('value')
                            });
                            // Insert radio before select box:
                            $p.append($checkbox);
                            // Insert a label:
                            $p.append(
                                    $("&lt;label class='optionLabel'/&gt;").attr('for', $checkbox.attr('id')).text($label.text())
                            );
                        }
                    });
                    $ul.before($p);
                    $ul.remove();
                });
            }
        }

        else {
            $('&lt;link rel="stylesheet" href="/resources/css/padiact/ro/'+padiact.id+'.css" type="text/css" /&gt;').appendTo('head');

            if ( $('.padiFormWrap select').length &gt; 0 ){
                //Get Exising Select Options
                $('.padiFormWrap select').each(function(i, select){
                    var $select = $(select);
                    $select.find('option').each(function(j, option){
                        var $option = $(option);
                        // Create a radio:
                        var $radio = $('&lt;input type="radio" id="'+j+'"/&gt;');
                        // Set name and value:
                        $radio.attr('name', $select.attr('name')).attr('value', $option.val());
                        // Insert radio before select box:
                        $select.before($radio);
                        // Insert a label:
                        $select.before(
                          $("&lt;label class='optionLabel'/&gt;").attr('for', $radio.attr('id')).text($option.text())
                        );
                    });
                    $select.remove();
                });
            }
        }
	}
}
  </script>

  <script type="text/javascript">
   function get_browser_version(){
        var N=navigator.appName, ua=navigator.userAgent, tem;
        var M=ua.match(/(opera|chrome|safari|firefox|msie)\/?\s*(\.?\d+(\.\d+)*)/i);
        if(M &amp;&amp; (tem= ua.match(/version\/([\.\d]+)/i))!= null) M[2]= tem[1];
        M=M? [M[1], M[2]]: [N, navigator.appVersion, '-?'];
        return parseInt(M[1]);
    }
    $(document).ready(function(){
        if ($.cookie('oldBrowserIHaveBeenWarned') != 'yes' &amp;&amp; (($.browser.msie &amp;&amp; get_browser_version() &lt; 8) || ($.browser.mozilla &amp;&amp; get_browser_version() &lt; 3))) {
            $.blockUI({
                'message': $('#compatibility-popup'),
                'css': {
                    'cursor': 'auto',
                    'height': '407px',
                    'width': '491px',
                    'textAlign': 'left',
                    'border': 'none',
                    'backgroundColor': 'none',
                    'zIndex':9998,
                    'top': '50%',
                    'marginTop': '-203px'
                },
                'overlayCSS':  {
                    'cursor': 'auto',
                    'backgroundColor':'#e8e8e8',
                    'opacity': 0.9,
                    'zIndex':9998
                }
            });
            window.closePopUp = function() {
                $.unblockUI();
                return false;
            }

            $('.close-old-warning').on('click',function(e){
                $.cookie('oldBrowserIHaveBeenWarned','yes');
                closePopUp();
            });
            $('.blockUI.blockOverlay').click(function(){
                $.cookie('oldBrowserIHaveBeenWarned','yes');
            });
        }
    });
  </script>
